Timeline of Legends media
687059

This timeline is intended to list narrative-based Legends media by an in-universe chronology. The list includes films, television episodes, novels, comic books, short stories, video games, and other promotional material. Placement of media in the timeline observes in-universe chronology. In order to ensure reliability, sources must always be included when providing dates. The order of chronology within the timeline adheres to the following criteria: *All entries are ordered based on the beginning of the "main events," as defined in the Layout Guide. *Official sources for timeline placements are always given precedent over "logical" placements. *The order in which full adaptations are listed are as follows: Film, Novel, Junior Novel, Young Readers, Graphic Novel, Comic Book Miniseries. *Short story anthologies are broken down into individual titles and placed according to story-specific dates. :Ω - Original date was modified by The Clone Wars project as indicated by the The Essential Reader's Companion :&dagger; - Exact placement unknown :‡ - Exact placement needs confirmation relative to other media :Legends media that is not listed on the timeline indicates that the Battle of Alderaan occurs four years after the Battle of Bothawui. According to Timeline 5: The Battle of Bothawui the Battle of Bothawui occurs eighteen years before the Treaty of Coruscant, which, as seen in The Old Republic: Deceived, is proposed and ratified in 3653 BBY. Thusly, the Battle of Bothawui takes place in 3671 BBY, and the Battle of Alderaan occurs four years later, in 3667 BBY. ||- class="promotional" | P || || 2010-06-14 |- class="short" | 3667 BBY ||- class="comic" | 22 BBY states that General Grievous attempted to capture the planet Kothlis between the battle of JanFathal (from The Clone Wars: No Prisoners) and the battle of Nexus Ortai (from The Clone Wars: Shipyards of Doom). Although Grievous was involved in the later battle on Kothlis as depicted in Clone Wars Gambit: Stealth, The Essential Reader's Companion and date No Prisoners and Shipyards of Doom to 22 BBY respectively, and The Essential Reader's Companion instead dates Clone Wars Gambit: Stealth to 21 BBY. Thus, The Official Star Wars Fact File Part 29 must instead be referring to the battle from The Clone Wars: The Wind Raiders of Taloraan, and the battle must occur in 22 BBY as well. ||- class="comic" | C || The Clone Wars: The Wind Raiders of Taloraan || 2009-05-27 |- class="comic" | 22 BBY ||- class="comic" | C || The Clone Wars: Shipyards of Doom || 2008-09-24 |- class="short" | 22 BBY ||- class="short" | SS || Ω *Originally dated to month 3 ABG || 2004-01-13 |- class="comic" | 22 BBY ||- class="comic" | C || &dagger; *Month 3 ABG || 2007-06-20 |- class="novel" | 22 BBY ||- class="novel" | N || Republic Commando: Hard Contact Ω *Originally dated to month 3 ABG || 2004-10-26 |- class="short" | 22 BBY ||- class="short" | SS || Ω *Originally dated to month 4 ABG || 2005-03-28 |- class="comic" | 22 BBY ||- class="comic" | C || &dagger; *Month 5 ABG || 2004-07-07 |- class="comic" | 22 BBY ||- class="comic" | C || &dagger; *Month 5 ABG || 2004-05-01 |- class="comic" | 22 BBY ||- class="comic" | C || &dagger; *Month 5 ABG || 2004-11-17 |- class="novel" | 22 BBY ||- class="novel" | N || Shatterpoint Ω *Originally dated to month 6 ABG || 2003-06-03 |- class="short" | 22 BBY ||- class="short" | SS || Ω *Takes place during the events of Shatterpoint. As the Living Force adventure "Below the Belt: Philology" moved the campaign forward ten years to the Time of the Clone Wars, and the adventure "Night Eyes: Night's Homecoming" established that by Year 4 of the campaign over a year had elapsed since the events of "Philology", this adventure can therefore be dated to circa 20 BBY. ||- class="adventure" | RPG || &dagger; Month 12 ABE. || 1998-10-28 |- class="comic" | c. 5 ABYStar Wars 108: Forever Crimson is set shortly after the end of the Nagai–Tof War, which The New Essential Chronology places in 4 ABY. In this issue, Leia Organa explains that the events of Star Wars (1977) 50 happened "years ago". As a result, the events of Star Wars 108: Forever Crimson must take place at least two years after the events of Star Wars 50: The Crimson Forever, which are set in 3 ABY. 2002-12-11 |- class="novel" | 35 ABYThe Essential Reader's Companion establishes that the Dark Nest trilogy begins in 35 BBY and ends in 36 BBY, while the text of Dark Nest II: The Unseen Queen dates its events to one year after those of Dark Nest I: The Joiner King, the first book of the trilogy. Therefore, the events of The Joiner King must take place in 35 BBY, and those of The Unseen Queen and the subsequent Dark Nest III: The Swarm War in 36 BBY. ||- class="novel" | N || Dark Nest I: The Joiner King || 2005-07-26 |- class="novel" | 36 ABY ||- class="novel" | N || Dark Nest II: The Unseen Queen || 2005-09-27 |- class="novel" | 36 ABY ||- class="novel" | N || Dark Nest III: The Swarm War || 2005-12-27 |} {|width="100%" class="sortable" !
